<h1 style='margin-left:21.25pt;text-indent:-21.25pt;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo1'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>1.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>说明</span></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.25pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.02;
line-height:115%'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>SnBuilderController</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>实现对</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>SnBuilderService</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>进行简单的封装，对外提供</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>We</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri'>服务的</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>API</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.25pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.02;
line-height:115%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>本模块以独立的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>Web</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>服务</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>(rest)</span><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>对外提供功能。</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:115%'>SnBuilderService</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri'>实现了</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>ISnBuilderService</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>接口具体的业务逻辑功能，并通过注入的方式提供给</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>SnBuilderController</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>或其他模块调用；</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>SnBuilderController</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>对</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>SnBuilderService</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>进行简单的封装，对外提供</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>We</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri'>服务的</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>API</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.25pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.02;
line-height:115%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:

lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.0pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.0'><span

lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:21.25pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.77'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri'>包含表达式引擎相关说明。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-hansi-font-family:宋体'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h1 style='margin-left:21.25pt;text-indent:-21.25pt;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo1'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>2.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>交互图</span></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:115%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri'>参见《</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>M000</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>示例服务设计</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>.doc</span><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>》典型调用图。</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:115%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h1 style='margin-left:21.25pt;text-indent:-21.25pt;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo1'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>3.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>界面设计</span></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.25pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.02;
line-height:115%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>无</span><span

<h1 style='margin-left:21.25pt;text-indent:-21.25pt;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo1'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>4.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>功能设计</span></h1>

<h2 style='margin-left:1.0cm;text-indent:-1.0cm;mso-list:l4 level2 lfo1'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>4.1.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria'>公式定义</span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:21.2pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.02'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>公式生成使用</span><span
lang=EN-US>Java 8</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>最新的</span><span lang=EN-US>Nashorn</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>引擎（官方参考文档：</span><span
lang=EN-US>http://www.oracle.com/technetwork/articles/java/jf14-nashorn-2126515.html?ssSourceSiteId=ocomen</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，简单使用说明：</span><span
lang=EN-US>http://www.jb51.net/article/92138.htm</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>），由服务器端执行</span><span
lang=EN-US>JavaScript</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>脚本。本模块向</span><span lang=EN-US>JavaScript</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>中注入了宿主对象</span><span
lang=EN-US>$</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（模仿</span><span lang=EN-US>jquery</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>的设计，使用</span><span
lang=EN-US>$</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>作为变量名）。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:21.2pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.02'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>编号生成将分两个阶段，第一阶段用于生成分类值，第二阶段用于生成最终编号。除</span><span
lang=EN-US>N</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>方法外，其它方法不区分所处阶段。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:21.3pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.02'><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>由于服务端使用</span><span lang=EN-US>JavaScript</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>表达式语法，因此表达式可以兼容服务端与客户端。</span><span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<h2 style='margin-left:1.0cm;text-indent:-1.0cm;mso-list:l4 level2 lfo1'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>4.2.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
lang=EN-US>$</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Cambria;
mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria'>对象封装</span></h2>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;

  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>字段或方法</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;

  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>类型</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;

  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>描述</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:1'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.print(msg)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>void</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>将消息内容输出到控制台（浏览器使用</span><span lang=EN-US>console.log</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>，服务器使用</span><span lang=EN-US>System.out.println</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>并写入到</span><span lang=EN-US>&lt;</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>日志根目录</span><span
  lang=EN-US>&gt;/scriptLog/{yyyy-MM-dd}.log</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>文件）</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:2'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;
  font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;color:#444444;background:white'>$.messager</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>void</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>简单消息框封装类。仅前端表达式有效</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:3'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;
  font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;color:#444444;background:white'>$.messager.progress(param)<o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>当</span><span lang=EN-US>param</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>为</span><span lang=EN-US>&quot;bar&quot;</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>时返回进度条控件；</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>其它情况返回空</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>显示一个进度提示框（进度可控制）【<span style='color:red'>仅前端表达式有效，当前实现需要</span></span><span
  lang=EN-US style='color:red'>easyui</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:red'>支持</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>】。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>param:</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>取值有：</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>一、初始化信息</span><span lang=EN-US
  style='color:#0070C0'>{title:</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#0070C0'>显示在标题栏的文字</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='color:#0070C0'>,msg:</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#0070C0'>提示文字</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='color:#0070C0'>,text:</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#0070C0'>在进度条上的文字</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='color:#0070C0'>,</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;color:#0070C0;background:white'>interval</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='color:#0070C0'>:</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#0070C0'>进度条推进时间间隔</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='color:#0070C0'>(ms)}</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>其中</span><span lang=EN-US>title</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;
  color:#444444;background:white'> </span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;
  font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;mso-hansi-font-family:Helvetica;
  mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#444444;background:white'>默认为空，空表示不显示标题栏；</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;
  color:#444444;background:white'>text </span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#444444;background:white'>默认为</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;
  color:#444444;background:white'>undefined</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#444444;background:white'>，如果指定为</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;
  color:#444444;background:white'>undefined</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#444444;background:white'>，则进度条上显示百分比文字；</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;
  color:#444444;background:white'>interval </span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#444444;background:white'>默认为</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;
  color:#444444;background:white'>300</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#444444;background:white'>，设为</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;
  color:#444444;background:white'>0</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;
  font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;mso-hansi-font-family:Helvetica;
  mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#444444;background:white'>，则不自动推进进度条。</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;
  color:#444444;background:white'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;mso-hansi-font-family:Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:
  Helvetica;color:#444444;background:white'>二、</span><span lang=EN-US
  style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;
  color:#0070C0;background:white'>&quot;close&quot;</span><span
  style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#444444;
  background:white'>，关闭此进度提示框</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;color:#444444;background:white'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;mso-hansi-font-family:Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:
  Helvetica;color:#444444;background:white'>三、</span><span lang=EN-US
  style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;
  color:#0070C0;background:white'>&quot;bar&quot;</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#444444;background:white'>，获得</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;
  color:#444444;background:white'>progressbar</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#444444;background:white'>（进度条控件，可通过返回控件使用</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;
  color:#444444;background:white'>getValue/setValue</span><span
  style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#444444;
  background:white'>控制进度）：</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;color:#444444;background:white'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:15.75pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5'><span
  lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;
  color:#444444;background:white'>var bar=$.messager.progress(&quot;bar&quot;)</span><span
  lang=EN-US>;</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:15.75pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5'><span
  lang=EN-US>bar.progressbar(&quot;setValue&quot;,30);</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:#538135'>//</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri;color:#538135'>也可重新设置进度条高度：</span><span lang=EN-US style='color:#538135'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:15.75pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.5'><span
  lang=EN-US>bar.progressbar({height:4});</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shapetype

  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:4'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;

  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>显示遮罩提示框。【<span style='color:red'>仅前端表达式有效，当前实现需要</span></span><span
  lang=EN-US style='color:red'>easyui</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:red'>支持</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>】</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>param</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，显示的提示信息（支持</span><span
  lang=EN-US>html</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>格式），如果为空或不传参数，则表过关闭遮罩提示框。如：</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.messager.mask(&quot;</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>正在查询，请稍候</span><span lang=EN-US>...&quot;);</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:#538135'>//</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri;color:#538135'>在查询完成后调用</span><span lang=EN-US style='color:#538135'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.messager.mask();</span></p>

  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>当前月份的日号值，如果是一号到九号，高位不会补零。</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>

 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:13'>

  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:

  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>将日期格式的值转换成日期值对象。识别</span><span lang=EN-US>timestmap</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>的整数、</span><span lang=EN-US>yyyy-MM-dd HH:mm:ss</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>（包括</span><span lang=EN-US>/</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>分隔符）、</span><span
  lang=EN-US>yyyy</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>年</span><span lang=EN-US>MM</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>月</span><span lang=EN-US>dd</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>日</span><span
  lang=EN-US> HH</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>时</span><span lang=EN-US>mm</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>分</span><span lang=EN-US>ss</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>秒、</span><span
  lang=EN-US>Mon Jul 25 2017 04:05:23 GMT+0800</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>、</span><span
  lang=EN-US>yyyyMMdd</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>、</span><span lang=EN-US>yyyyMMddHHmmss</span></p>

  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>字符串</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>获得指定分类的最大流水号值。仅在编号公式表达式中使用。其它表达式内，调用此方法将返回指定长度的</span><span
  lang=EN-US>0</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>值。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>参数：</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>numberLength</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>【必须】：数字，指定生成编号的长度。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>type</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【可选】：字符串，用于生成最终编号前替换流水号的类型值。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>返回值：【第一阶段】“替换流水号值”的分类值；【第二阶段】当前分类下的最大流水号。</span></p>

  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;

  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;

  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>在表单加载完成后执行的代码。（表单加载完成，不保证子表单控件内的数据加载完成）</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:red'>此方法仅适用于前端表达式，且仅在</span><span

  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:red'>架构，可以使用</span><span

 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:18'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.F</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>对象</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>表单对象，用于访问表单数据。对应表单引擎接口“</span><span
  lang=EN-US>IFormService</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体'>”</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体'>（详细说明参见《<span lang=EN-US>iBase2.0[M0211]</span>表单处理引擎<span
  lang=EN-US>.doc</span>》）</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:19'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.F.getFieldValue(String formDomainName)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>具体值类型</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>获取某个字段值（</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#141414;background:white'>可获取按钮或静态文本</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;
  color:#141414;background:white'>[</span><span lang=EN-US>innerText</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;
  color:#141414;background:white'>]</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;
  font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;mso-hansi-font-family:Helvetica;
  mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#141414;background:white'>的显示文本内容</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>）。类型：</span><span lang=EN-US>Object</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，根据字段类型返回不同值类型，一般有：字符串、整数、小数、日期等。<span
  style='color:red'>如果匹配到多个字段（主要是没有传入</span></span><span lang=EN-US
  style='color:red'>rid</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:red'>的子表单），则返回数组，每个元素是形如</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='color:red'>{id:xxx,value:yyy}</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:red'>的对象（</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='color:red'>id</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:red'>指所取数据的记录</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='color:red'>mrid</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:red'>，</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='color:red'>value</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:red'>为所取字段值）；如果获取的是子表单控件（未指定子表单内的字段时），则返回记录数组，每个元素是一条子表单数据，是表字段值对，形如</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='color:red'>{JOB_SA.SYS_MRID:xxx,JOB_SA.F1:yyy, JOB_SA$GA.F2:zzz,
  ...}</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>参数：</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>formDomainName</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>，字段唯一名。格式：“库表名</span><span lang=EN-US>$</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>组名</span><span lang=EN-US>@RID.</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>字段名</span><span
  lang=EN-US>&gt;</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>子表单字段”，如：</span><span lang=EN-US>JOB_A.FMJ</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>、</span><span lang=EN-US>JOB_A$old.FMJ</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>、</span><span
  lang=EN-US>JOB_A@1df809ae-8a81-dc23-132038ae.F1&gt;JOB_B.SJ</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>、</span><span lang=EN-US>JOB_A.F1&gt;JOB_B.SJ</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>其中</span><span lang=EN-US>SYS_MRID</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>的表名可以是子表单关联的任何一个表名（以后改进，也可省略表名）。</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:20'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.F.getFieldDicText(String
  formDomainName)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>字符串</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>获取字典项控件的显示值（</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#141414;background:white'>可获取按钮或静态文本的显示文本内容</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;
  color:#141414;background:white'>[innerHtml]</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>），否则返回字段值。</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:21'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.F.getFieldDicValue(String
  formDomainName)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>字符串</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>获取字典项控件的内部值，否则返回字段值</span> <span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>。</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:22'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.F.setFieldValue(String formDomainName,
  Object fieldValue, <span style='color:red'>int sType</span>)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>为指定字段设置值（</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#141414;background:white'>可改变按钮或静态文本的显示文本内容①</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;
  color:#141414;background:white'>[innerText]</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#141414;background:white'>）</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>。如果通过字段名匹配到多个字段，依具</span><span lang=EN-US>fieldValue</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>值类型分三种处理：②如果是基本类型（不包含</span><span lang=EN-US>id/value</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>属性），则所有匹配字段设置相同的值；如果是自定义</span><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
  lang=EN-US>Object</span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>类型</span></b><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，再分为③记录对象，形如：</span><span lang=EN-US>{JOB_A.SYS_MRID:&quot;&quot;,
  JOB_A.F1:&quot;&quot;, JOB_A$old.F2:&quot;&quot;, JOB_B.F11:&quot;&quot;}</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>）或<b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>其数组</b>，则匹配字段的记录</span><span
  lang=EN-US>mrid</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>与此对象</span><span lang=EN-US>mrid</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>相同的对象属性值赋给匹配字段，如果此时</span><span lang=EN-US>mrid</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>未找到，或为空，则添加一条记录；如果是④</span><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
  lang=EN-US>{id:&quot;&quot;,value:&quot;&quot;}</span></b><b
  style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>的</span><span lang=EN-US>Object</span></b><b
  style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>对象或其数组</span></b><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>，则匹配字段的记录</span><span lang=EN-US>mrid</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>与此对象</span><span
  lang=EN-US>id</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>相同的对象属性值赋给匹配字段，如果此时</span><span lang=EN-US>mrid</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>未找到，或为空，则添加一条记录。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>如果子表单内的某个字段也是子表单，赋值格式如下：</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>{</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>JOB_A.SYS_MRID:&quot;&quot;,</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>JOB_A.F1:&quot;sadf&quot;,</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>JOB_B.F11:[</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>{JOB_SS.SYS_MRID:&quot;&quot;,JOB_SS.FAA:&quot;11&quot;,JOB_SS.FBB:&quot;22&quot;},</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>{JOB_SS.SYS_MRID:&quot;&quot;,JOB_SS.FAA:&quot;##&quot;,JOB_SS.FBB:&quot;**&quot;},</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>{JOB_SS.SYS_MRID:&quot;&quot;,JOB_SS.FAA:&quot;aa&quot;,JOB_SS.FBB:&quot;bb&quot;}</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>]</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>}</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>如果是为下拉控件赋值，⑤值形如</span><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
  normal'><span lang=EN-US>{text:&quot;&quot;,id:&quot;&quot;,parentid&quot;&quot;,children:[]}</span></b><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>的</span><span lang=EN-US>Object</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>对象（</span><span
  lang=EN-US>text</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>为下拉选项的显示文本，</span><span lang=EN-US>id</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>为下拉选项的标识值，</span><span lang=EN-US>parentid</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>为多级下拉框时所结附的父级节点</span><span lang=EN-US>id</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>，</span><span lang=EN-US>children</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>为多级下拉框时所包含的子项节点），先向下拉框添加项，然后选中此项。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:red'>sType(</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri;color:red'>可选</span><span lang=EN-US style='color:red'>)</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri;color:red'>：要填充的批量子表单数据结构一致时，传入</span><span lang=EN-US
  style='color:red'>1</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:red'>可加快填充的速度，默认不传。</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:23'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.F.setFieldDicText(String
  formDomainName, String text)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>为指定字段设置对应的文本项（</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#141414;background:white'>可改变按钮或静态文本的显示文本内容</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;
  color:#141414;background:white'>[innerHtml]</span><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#141414;background:white'>）</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>，否则设置指定值。</span></p>
  </td>

 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:24'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.F.findSubForm(String formDomainName,
  Map filter)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>键值对数组</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>formDomainName</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>，指定要查找内部记录的子表单控件的字段唯一名；</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>filter</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，子表单内记录查找条件组（多个名值对以</span><span
  lang=EN-US>and</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>组合），如：</span><span lang=EN-US>{JOB_SS.FAA:&quot;11&quot;,JOB_SS.FBB:&quot;22&quot;}</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:red'>暂不支持子表单内子表单数据的查找。</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='color:red'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>返回找到的所有记录对象。</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:25'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.F.getSelectedSubForm(String
  formDomainName, bool bChecked)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>键值对数组</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>formDomainName</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>，指定要查找内部记录的子表单控件的字段唯一名（支持</span><span lang=EN-US>@@</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>前缀，指相对于当前打开子表单窗口）；</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>bChecked</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，是否获取勾选的记录（如果为</span><span
  lang=EN-US>true</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，则获取勾先的记录，</span><span lang=EN-US>false</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>，则获取当前高亮选中记录）。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>返回找到的所有记录对象。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:red'>此方法仅适用于前端表达式。</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='color:red'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:26'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.F.refreshSubForm(String formDomainName)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>重新加载子表单数据。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>formDomainName</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>，指定要刷新记录的子表单控件的字段唯一名</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:red'>此方法仅适用于前端表达式。</span></p>

 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:27'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;
  font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;color:#141414;background:white'>$.F.isInitSubForm(</span><span
  lang=EN-US>String formDomainName</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;color:#141414;background:white'>)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>布尔值</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>判断指定子表单控件是否正在初始化。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>返回：</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;color:#141414;background:white'>true</span><span
  style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#141414;
  background:white'>表示正在初始化，</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;color:#141414;background:white'>false</span><span
  style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:Helvetica;color:#141414;
  background:white'>表示已初始化完成</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:
  10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;color:#141414;background:white'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Helvetica;mso-hansi-font-family:Helvetica;mso-bidi-font-family:
  Helvetica;color:#141414;background:white'>子表单正在初始化，是指在控件从发出请求获取初始数据开始，到将返回的数据填充到控件并完成的过程。</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;font-family:"Helvetica",sans-serif;
  color:#141414;background:white'><o:p></o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:red'>此方法仅适用于前端表达式。</span></p>

  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:40'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;

  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>获取登录用户名。</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:41'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.O.getUserQua(uid,mark)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>用户身份值</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>获取指定用户</span><span lang=EN-US>id</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>的身份信息，如果不是用户</span><span lang=EN-US>id</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，则返回</span><span
  lang=EN-US>0</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>参数：</span><span lang=EN-US>uid</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>，用户</span><span lang=EN-US>id</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>；</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>mark</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>，掩码值（由于身份标识是按位组合，因此可以用于获取需要的位，</span><span lang=EN-US>1</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>【</span><span lang=EN-US>B0</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>】：部门负责人，</span><span
  lang=EN-US>2</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【</span><span lang=EN-US>B1</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>】：部门联系人，</span><span lang=EN-US>4</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【</span><span
  lang=EN-US>B2</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>】：部门管理员）。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>比如：</span><span lang=EN-US>$.O.getUserQua('aabb-dd',1)==1</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>，表示要获取部门负责人位，返回</span><span lang=EN-US>1</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>表示此位有效；</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>又如：</span><span lang=EN-US>$.O.getUserQua('aabb-dd',5)==4</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>，表示要获取部门负责人位和部门管理员位，返回</span><span lang=EN-US>4</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>表示部门管理员位有效。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>返回：整数（返回的值表示哪些位有效：</span><span lang=EN-US>0=</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>无任何位有效，</span><span lang=EN-US>1=</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>第</span><span
  lang=EN-US>0</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>位有效，</span><span lang=EN-US>2=</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>第</span><span lang=EN-US>1</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>位有效，</span><span
  lang=EN-US>3=</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>第</span><span lang=EN-US>0</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>和</span><span lang=EN-US>1</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>位有效，</span><span
  lang=EN-US>4=</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>第</span><span lang=EN-US>2</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>位有效，</span><span lang=EN-US>5=</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>第</span><span
  lang=EN-US>0</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>和</span><span lang=EN-US>2</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>位有效，</span><span lang=EN-US>6=</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>第</span><span
  lang=EN-US>1</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>和</span><span lang=EN-US>2</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>位有效，</span><span lang=EN-US>7=</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>第</span><span
  lang=EN-US>0</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>、</span><span lang=EN-US>1</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>和</span><span lang=EN-US>2</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>位有效。依此类推）</span></p>
  </td>

  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>根据组织项的内部代码获取组织项对象</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:45'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;

  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>组织项对象</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>根据组织项的层次名获取组织项对象（从上向下找，如果层次中的名称找不到组织项，将返回空）</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>如：</span><span lang=EN-US>$.O.getOrganInfoByName(&quot;</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>南方数码</span><span lang=EN-US>/</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>研发中心</span><span
  lang=EN-US>/</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>研发部</span><span lang=EN-US>/</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>经理</span><span lang=EN-US>/&quot;) </span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>获取的是部门或岗位、</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.O.getOrganInfoByName(&quot;[</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>经理</span><span lang=EN-US>]&quot;) </span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>获取的是角色、</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.O.getOrganInfoByName(&quot;</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>南方数码</span><span lang=EN-US>/</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>研发中心</span><span
  lang=EN-US>/</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>研发部</span><span lang=EN-US>/</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>工程师</span><span lang=EN-US>/</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>张三</span><span
  lang=EN-US>&quot;) </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>获取的是人员</span></p>
  </td>

 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:46'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;

  <p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span lang=EN-US>$.O.getOwnerDept(uid)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;

  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>组织项对象</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>获取直接部门，如果是人员，获取首要岗位的直接部门。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>类型：</span><span lang=EN-US>OrganInfoLocal</span></p>

  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>组织项对象</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>获取指定级别的上级部门（</span><span lang=EN-US>status</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>字段描述级别）。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US>uid</span></b><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>：组织结构</span><span lang=EN-US>ID</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>；</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US>cls</span></b><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>：级别值，有效值如下（值越小级别越高）</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>2</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>：单位或公司节点</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>11</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>：一级部门节点</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>12</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>：二级部门节点</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>13</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>：三级部门节点</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>14</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>：四级部门节点</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>15</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>：五级部门节点</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>获取的部门级别满足如下条件：组织项级别值（</span><span lang=EN-US>status</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>）大于</span><span lang=EN-US>1</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，且小于等于指定级别值</span><span
  lang=EN-US>cls</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>返回指定级别的部门对象。若</span><span lang=EN-US>uid</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>是人员，获取的是首要岗位满足条件的上级部门。从直接部门向上查找，直到找到的部门级别等于或高于指定级别的部门。</span></p>
  </td>

 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:54'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;

  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.X(administratorCode)</span></p>

  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
