  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>获取行政区划信息。类型：</span><span lang=EN-US>AdministrativeDivision[]</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>参数：</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>administratorCode</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>【必须】：字符串，行政区划代码</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>返回值：</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>一个行政区划</span><span lang=EN-US>AdministrativeDivision</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>的数组，第一项为省，第二项为市、第三项为县、第四项为乡、第五项为村、第六项为组、第七项为小组直到</span><span
  lang=EN-US>administratorCode</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>指定的行政区划级别（最多</span><span lang=EN-US>7</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>项）。说明见表后（注</span><span lang=EN-US>1</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>）。</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:55'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.C(catalogCode, showValue)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>字典对象数组</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>获取字典项信息。类型：</span><span lang=EN-US>CodeDict[]</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>参数</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>catalogCode</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【必须】：代码字典的分类码或显示文本，</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>showValue</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【必须】：字典项代码或显示文本。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>返回值：字典对象数组。如果未找到，返回长度为</span><span lang=EN-US>0</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>的数组。说明见表后（注</span><span lang=EN-US>2</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>）</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:56'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.S(catalog,key)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>字符串</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>获得指定分类的系统配置项内容。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>catalog</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【必须】，分类名</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>key</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【必须】，配置项。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>返回：配置值</span><span lang=EN-US>(</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>如果未获取到，返回空。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>此方法先用本系统</span><span lang=EN-US>ID</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>关联的配置查找，如果找不到，再忽略系统</span><span lang=EN-US>ID</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>查找（即找到任何一个同分类同名的配置）。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>如：</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.S(&quot;</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>单位信息</span><span
  lang=EN-US>&quot;,&quot;</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>所属行政区</span><span lang=EN-US>&quot;)</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:57'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.buildNo(expFla)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>字符串</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>通过指定的编号公式（使用编号公式定义模块定义需要的公式），生成唯一编号。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>expFla</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【必须】，编号公式名</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>返回：根据编号公式定义的格式生成的唯一编号值。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>如：查</span><span lang=EN-US>[2014]012</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>号</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:58'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.execsql (dsName,sql1,param1,sql2,param2,sql3,param3)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Map</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>条件执行</span><span lang=EN-US>sql</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>语句：先执行</span><span lang=EN-US>sql1</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，成功且有返回值则执行</span><span
  lang=EN-US>sql2</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，否则</span><span lang=EN-US>(</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>不出异常时</span><span lang=EN-US>)</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>执行</span><span
  lang=EN-US>sql3</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>dsName:</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>数据源查询服务配置名，用于支持多数据源的查询（暂未使用）</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>sql1</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【必须】</span><span
  lang=EN-US>:</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>语句命名（为了安全，不直接写</span><span lang=EN-US>sql</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>语句，而是由单独模块定义</span><span lang=EN-US>sql</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>并命名，通过命名找到</span><span lang=EN-US>sql</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>语句内容）</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>param1:</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>所执行语句的参数名值对的</span><span
  lang=EN-US>Map</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>对象。依据命名所对应的</span><span lang=EN-US>sql</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>语句中的参数定义方式，支持占位符参数</span> <span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>如：</span><span lang=EN-US>{&quot;?1&quot;:&quot;#date#&quot;,&quot;?2&quot;:1,&quot;?3&quot;:&quot;1-23-4&quot;}</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>，及与命名参数</span> <span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>如：</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>{&quot;regdate&quot;:&quot;#date#&quot;,&quot;mj&quot;:1,&quot;rid&quot;:&quot;1-23-4&quot;}</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>sql2/param2</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>、</span><span
  lang=EN-US>sql3/param3</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>：说明同上，<span style='color:red'>注：如果没有执行语句，则设置为</span></span><span
  lang=EN-US style='color:red'>null</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:red'>。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>返回每条</span><span lang=EN-US>sql</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>语句的执行结果名值对的</span><span lang=EN-US>Map</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>对象。</span><span
  lang=EN-US>key</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>名分别为</span><span lang=EN-US>“sql1”</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>，</span><span lang=EN-US>“sql2”</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，</span><span
  lang=EN-US>“sql3”</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，值为对应</span><span lang=EN-US>sql</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>语句的结果：</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>如果是</span><span lang=EN-US>select</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>语句，返回</span><span lang=EN-US>List&lt;Map&lt;String,Object&gt;&gt;</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>格式的记录集（</span><span lang=EN-US>Map</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>指一条记录结果，</span><span
  lang=EN-US>Key</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>为字段名，</span><span lang=EN-US>Value</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>为字段值）；</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>如果是</span><span lang=EN-US>insert</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>、</span><span lang=EN-US>update</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>、</span><span
  lang=EN-US>delete</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>语句，返回影响的记录数。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>若对应某条语句未执行，相应结果为</span><span lang=EN-US>null</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>。</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:59'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.execproc(dsName,procName,inParam,outParam)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>Map</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>执行存贮过程。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>dsName:</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>数据源查询服务配置名，用于支持多数据源的查询（暂未使用）</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>procName</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【必须】：存贮过程名</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>inParam</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>：输入参数，名值对的</span><span
  lang=EN-US>Map</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>对象（但只支持命名参数的写法，不支持占位符参数）</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>outParam</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>：输出参数，名值对的</span><span
  lang=EN-US>Map</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>对象（也只支持命名参数的写法），每项参数的值为返回结果类型的描述字符串。如：</span><span
  lang=EN-US>{&quot;no&quot;:&quot;int&quot;}</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>varchar</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（字符串）、</span><span
  lang=EN-US>clob</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（大文本内容）：将返回字符串值；</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>int</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（整数）：将返回整数值；</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>double</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（浮点小数）、</span><span
  lang=EN-US>decimal</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（定点小数）：将返回小数值；</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>datetime</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（日期）：将返回日期值（时间戳）；</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>blob</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（大二进制块）：将返回</span><span
  lang=EN-US>base64</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>编码的二进制值；</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>cursor</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（游标，只能一个）：将返回</span><span
  lang=EN-US>List&lt;Map&lt;String,Object&gt;&gt;</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>格式的记录集（</span><span
  lang=EN-US>Map</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>指一条记录结果，</span><span lang=EN-US>Key</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>为字段名，</span><span lang=EN-US>Value</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>为字段值）。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>注：为了兼容不同数据库存贮过程返回记录集的方式不同（</span><span
  lang=EN-US>Oracle</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>通过输出参数返回，</span><span lang=EN-US>mysql/sqlserver</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>通过查询语句返回），应统一按输出参数的方式调用（内部会正确处理通过查询语句返回的情况）。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>返回存贮过程的输出参数名值对</span><span lang=EN-US>Map</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>对象（</span><span lang=EN-US>Key</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>为参数名）</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:60'>
  <td width=187 valign=top style='width:140.1pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.batchsql(dsName,arrSqlInfo)</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=66 valign=top style='width:49.6pt;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>List</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=366 valign=top style='width:274.7pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>执行批量查询</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>dsName:</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>数据源查询服务配置名，用于支持多数据源的查询（暂未使用）</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>arrSqlInfo</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【必须】：查询信息数组，每个元素是</span><span
  lang=EN-US>SqlInfo</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>对象：</span><span lang=EN-US>{sql:</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>语句命名</span><span lang=EN-US>,param:[</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>参数名值对的</span><span
  lang=EN-US>Map</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>对象列表</span><span lang=EN-US>]} </span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>（参见</span><span lang=EN-US>execsql</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>相应参数说明）</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>返回每条</span><span lang=EN-US>sql</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>语句返回的记录集数组：</span><span lang=EN-US>List&lt;List&lt;</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>记录集</span><span lang=EN-US>&gt;&gt;</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span></span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>其中第一层数组元素是各条</span><span lang=EN-US>sql</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>语句的返回值数组（与传入的</span><span lang=EN-US>sql</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>语句顺序对应）；</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span></span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>第二层数组元素是每条</span><span lang=EN-US>sql</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>语句内不同组参数的返回的记录集结果（与</span><span
  lang=EN-US>param</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>参数顺序对应，但一般只有一组参数）</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span></span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>记录集返回</span><span lang=EN-US>List&lt;Map&lt;String,Object&gt;&gt;</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>（</span><span lang=EN-US>Map</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>指一条记录结果，</span><span
  lang=EN-US>Key</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>为字段名，</span><span lang=EN-US>Value</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>为字段值）</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>

  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>dsName:</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>数据源查询服务配置名，用于支持多数据源的查询（暂未使用）</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>arrSqlInfo</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【必须】：查询信息数组，每个元素是</span><span
  lang=EN-US>SqlInfo</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>语句返回的受影响记录数：</span><span lang=EN-US>List&lt;int[]&gt;</span><span

  Calibri'>。</span></p>

  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>其中第一层数组元素是各条</span><span lang=EN-US>sql</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>语句的返回值数组（与传入的</span><span lang=EN-US>sql</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>语句顺序对应）；</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span></span><span

  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>语句内不同组参数的返回结果（与</span><span

  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>参数顺序对应，每一项的值表示此参数下执行导致的影响记录数）</span></p>

  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>行政区划级别名</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:6;mso-yfti-lastrow:yes'>
  <td width=140 valign=top style='width:104.65pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>ad.S</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=76 valign=top style='width:2.0cm;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>字符串</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=404 valign=top style='width:303.05pt;border-top:none;border-left:
  none;border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>内部标识码</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
</table>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>指定的行政区划代码按如下格式区分级别：</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:red'>XX</span><span
lang=EN-US> <span style='color:#0070C0'>XX</span> <span style='color:#00B050'>XX</span>
<span style='color:#BF8F00'>XXX</span> <span style='color:#7030A0'>XXX</span>
XXX XXX</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:red'>前两位描述省或直辖市</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，<span
style='color:#0070C0'>其后两位描述省下的地级市</span>，<span style='color:#00B050'>再后两位描述地级市下的区或县</span>，<span
style='color:#BF8F00'>再后三位描述区县下的街道或乡镇</span>，<span style='color:#7030A0'>再后三位描述乡镇下的村</span>，其后三位或六位是按业务所需定义（一般描述村下的生产组或自然村落、及生产组下的小组）</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（注</span><span lang=EN-US>2</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>）</span><span
lang=EN-US>$.C</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>返回值为一个数组，数组中的元素为</span><span lang=EN-US>CodeDict</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，该对象支持以下字段：</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt'>4.1.2 </span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>其它内置对象</span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:14.15pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.35'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>请参考官网文档</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt'>4.1.3 </span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>服务端表达式支持</span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>1.</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>服务端表达式与客户端不同的地方是，</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-indent:-21.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo5'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;
mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>²<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>可以通过</span><span
lang=EN-US>Java.type</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>引入系统内的类来使用系统功能：</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>var expSql = Java.type(&quot;com.southgis.ibase.extend.service.SqlService&quot;);
<span style='color:#538135'>//</span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#538135'>引入执行</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:#538135'>SQL</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#538135'>的</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:#538135'>java</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#538135'>类定义</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>var result = expSql.query('getResult',{&quot;?1&quot;:&quot;201701010001&quot;},0);
<span style='color:#538135'>//</span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#538135'>调用静态方法</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>var obj=new expSql(); <span
style='color:#538135'>//</span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#538135'>调用构造方法</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>var result=obj.query(‘getAllTask’); <span
style='color:#538135'>//</span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#538135'>调用对象方法</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>var IntArray =
Java.type(&quot;int[]&quot;);<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span><span
style='color:#538135'>//</span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#538135'>引入</span><span lang=EN-US
style='color:#538135'>Java</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#538135'>的整型数组定义</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>var array = new IntArray(5);</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>array[0] = 5;</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-indent:-21.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo5'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;
mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>²<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>或获取工作流引擎对象，调用引擎内的其它方法：</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>var wfService=$.W.unwarp(); <span
style='color:#538135'>//</span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#538135'>获取工作流引擎原始对象（仅服务端有效）</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>wfService.updateDataBaseByCondition(&quot;{\&quot;JOB_BASE.JID\&quot;:\&quot;201807250001\&quot;}&quot;,</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>    </span>&quot;{\&quot;JOB_BASE.STATUS\&quot;:10}&quot;);</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;text-indent:-21.0pt;mso-list:l0 level1 lfo5'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:Wingdings;
mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>²<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>以及通过名字获取</span><span
lang=EN-US>spring</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>注入对象：</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:#538135'>//</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
color:#538135'>使用注入的对象，调用其中的方法</span><span lang=EN-US style='color:#538135'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>var appUtil = Java.type(&quot;com.southgis.ibase.utils.webservice.ApplicationContextUtil&quot;);</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>var
objProcess=appUtil.getBean(&quot;processInstanceService&quot;);</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>objProcess.modifyProcessInstanceName(&quot;processId&quot;,&quot;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>新名字</span><span
lang=EN-US>&quot;,$.O.getUserId());</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>2.</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>表达式扩展支持</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>2.1 sql</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>执行类</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-para-margin-left:2.0gd'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>类名：</span><span
lang=EN-US>com.southgis.ibase.extend.service.SqlService</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-para-margin-left:2.0gd'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>该类提供对</span><span
lang=EN-US>sql</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>语句的原生执行具体方法如下：</span><span lang=EN-US><br>
1</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri'>，</span><span lang=EN-US>List&lt;?&gt; query(String sql,Integer type)</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:42.0pt;mso-para-margin-left:4.0gd'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>该方法，执行</span><span
lang=EN-US>sql</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>语句查询，参数</span><span lang=EN-US>sql</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>标识要执行的</span><span
lang=EN-US>sql</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>语句，</span><span lang=EN-US>type </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>返回结果类型。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='margin-left:42.0pt;mso-para-margin-left:
4.0gd;text-align:left;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span
lang=EN-US>type=0 </span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>返回结果期望是</span><span lang=EN-US>List&lt;Object[]&gt;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（其中列表中的每个元素是一条记录，记录字段值按</span><span
lang=EN-US>sql</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>语句的字段顺序排列）</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:42.0pt;mso-para-margin-left:4.0gd'><span
lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>tyype=1 </span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>返回结果期望是一个</span><span
lang=EN-US>List&lt;Map&gt;</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（其中列表中的每个元素是一条</span><span lang=EN-US>Map</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>描述的记录，</span><span
lang=EN-US>Key</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>为全大写的字段名，</span><span lang=EN-US>Value</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>为字段值）。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-para-margin-left:2.0gd'><span
lang=EN-US>2</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，</span><span lang=EN-US>int execute(String sql)</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-para-margin-left:2.0gd'><span
lang=EN-US><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>         </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>该方法用来，执行</span><span
lang=EN-US>sql</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>原生增，删，改，语句，返回结果大于</span><span lang=EN-US>0</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>则是执行成功，其他情况失败。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;mso-layout-grid-align:
none;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US>3</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，</span><span
lang=EN-US>Map&lt;String, Object&gt; procedure(String procName, Map&lt;String,
Object&gt; inputParamMap,Map&lt;String, String&gt; outParamsMap)</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='margin-left:42.0pt;mso-para-margin-left:
4.0gd;text-align:left;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span
lang=EN-US><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>         </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>该方法用来执行存储过程，参数</span><span
lang=EN-US>inputParamMap</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>存储过程需要的参数。</span><span lang=EN-US>Key</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>为参数名，</span><span
lang=EN-US>Value</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>为参数值。</span><span lang=EN-US>outParamsMap</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>存储过程返回参数项，</span><span
lang=EN-US>Key</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>为参数名，</span><span lang=EN-US>Value</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>为参数类型：</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='margin-left:42.0pt;mso-para-margin-left:
4.0gd;text-align:left;mso-layout-grid-align:none;text-autospace:none'><span
lang=EN-US><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>         </span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>          
</span>varchar</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（字符串）、</span><span lang=EN-US>clob</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（大文本内容）、</span><span
lang=EN-US>int</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（整数）、</span><span lang=EN-US>double</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（浮点小数）、</span><span
lang=EN-US>decimal</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（定点小数）、</span><span lang=EN-US>datetime</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（日期）、</span><span
lang=EN-US>blob</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（大二进制块）、</span><span lang=EN-US>cursor</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>（游标，此类型参数最多只能一个。用于提取记录集，对于不支持游标返回的数据库，参数名可随意定义）。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;mso-layout-grid-align:
none;text-autospace:none'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>注意：该方法在支持</span><span lang=EN-US>MySQL</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>的游标没有问题，但是在支持</span><span
lang=EN-US>oracle</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>带游标参数返回时，会出现问题，待后续升级。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left;mso-layout-grid-align:
none;text-autospace:none'><span lang=EN-US>2.2 web</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>服务</span><span
lang=EN-US>URL</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>请求类</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-para-margin-left:2.0gd'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>类名：</span><span
lang=EN-US>com.southgis.ibase.extend.service.RequestService</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:21.0pt;mso-para-margin-left:2.0gd'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>该类提供支持对</span><span
lang=EN-US>Http</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>请求的访问。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:39.0pt;mso-para-margin-left:2.0gd;
text-indent:-18.0pt;mso-list:l1 level1 lfo4'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>1，<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
lang=EN-US>String doRequest(String path){}</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:38.95pt;mso-para-margin-left:3.71gd'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>参数：</span><span
lang=EN-US>path</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>为你想访问的地址。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:38.95pt;mso-para-margin-left:3.71gd'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>以字符串的形式返回整个页面。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt'>4.1.4 </span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>客户端表达式支持</span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:14.15pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.35'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>客户端需要有特殊对象：</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>1.</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>可使用</span><span
lang=EN-US>JQuery</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>对象</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:10.5pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.0'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>使用</span><span
lang=EN-US>$</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>访问，如：</span><span lang=EN-US>$(“#ctrlId”).val()</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:10.5pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.0'><span
lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>2.</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>可以在表单全局属性内引入封装的</span><span
lang=EN-US>js</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>文件（这样可实现业务通用功能的按需加载）</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.getScript(&quot;</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>要加载的脚本文件</span><span
lang=EN-US>.js&quot;);</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>注意：因为</span><span lang=EN-US>script</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>文件加载到页面都是异步执行的，因此用此方法动态加载脚本文件时，不能在需要立即使用的场合。最佳加载位置是表单的“全局属性</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体'>”</span><span style='font-family:宋体'>中。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-no-proof:yes'><!--[if gte vml 1]><v:shape
 id="_x0000_i1027" type="#_x0000_t75" style='width:453.75pt;height:255.75pt;
 visibility:visible'>
 <v:imagedata src="iBase2.0%5bM0213%5d编号公式管理(表达式引擎)%20(1).files/image006.png"
  o:title=""/>
</v:shape><![endif]--><![if !vml]><img border=0 width=605 height=341
src="iBase2.0%5bM0213%5d编号公式管理(表达式引擎)%20(1).files/image006.png" v:shapes="_x0000_i1027"><![endif]></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>3.</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>客户端运行时对象：</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>$.client <span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>             </span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>      </span><span style='color:#00B050'>// </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
color:#00B050'>客户端环境对象，服务端脚本内为</span><span lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>null</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
color:#00B050'>。包含属性</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>.rootWindow<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>   </span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>     </span><span style='color:#00B050'>// </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
color:#00B050'>框架文档（</span><span lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>window</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
color:#00B050'>对象，可以调用打开页功能），包含属性</span><span lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>      </span></span><span lang=EN-US>.addTap(null,module)<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span><span
style='color:#00B050'>//</span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#00B050'>打开窗口信息对象，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>//module</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
color:#00B050'>对象的属性至少包含：</span><span lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>//{<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>//<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>moduleId: </span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#00B050'>唯一标识窗口（用于窗口定位）</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>,<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>// <span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>name: </span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#00B050'>窗口标题名</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>,<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>// <span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>pageUrl:</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#00B050'>窗口内容地址</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>//}</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>     </span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>.ctx<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>      
</span><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>    </span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span><span style='color:#00B050'>// </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
color:#00B050'>当前框架应用路径（如：</span><span lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>/mainWeb</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
color:#00B050'>）</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>     
</span>.userId<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>    </span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>   </span><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span><span
style='color:#00B050'>// </span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#00B050'>当前登录用户</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>Id</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>     
</span>.realName<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>   </span><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span><span
style='color:#00B050'>// </span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#00B050'>用户名称</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>     
</span>.systemId<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>   </span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>   </span><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span><span
style='color:#00B050'>// </span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#00B050'>当前登录子系统</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>Id</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>.currentFieldName <span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span><span
style='color:#00B050'>// </span></span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#00B050'>当前控件名，表单控件内表达式有效，其它地方为</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>null</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#00B050'>。如果是子表单，则控件名还带有子表单前缀（比如：</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>S-3-12-JOB_A.F1</span><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#00B050'>，其中“</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>S-3-12-</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-family:宋体;color:#00B050'>”</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#00B050'>表示当前子表单前缀，且父表单也是子表单，前缀为“</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>S-3-</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:
宋体;color:#00B050'>”</span><span style='font-family:宋体;color:#00B050'>）</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>.currentValue<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>   </span><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>   </span><span style='color:#00B050'>// </span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
color:#00B050'>当前控件值，表单控件内表达式有效，其它地方为</span><span lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>null<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>   </span></span><span lang=EN-US>.currentItem<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>      </span><span style='color:#00B050'>//</span></span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
color:#00B050'>当前下拉框控件有效，为选中项（可以有多项）的名值对：</span><span lang=EN-US
style='color:#00B050'>[{text:</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#00B050'>显示值</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>,id:</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#00B050'>内部值</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>},{…}]<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><s><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>.currentParentField<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span><span style='color:#00B050'>// </span></span></s><s><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
color:#00B050'>如果是子表单内的控件表达式，描述此子表单控件名及对应的记录</span><span lang=EN-US
style='color:#00B050'>Mrid</span></s><s><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#00B050'>，非子表单内为</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>null</span></s><s><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#00B050'>，如果有嵌套，则包含所有层次的子表单控件名以</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>&gt;</span></s><s><span style='font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:#00B050'>分隔（比如：</span><span
lang=EN-US style='color:#00B050'>JOB_A@123.F1&gt;JOB_S1@2345.FN</span></s><s><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;
color:#00B050'>）。</span><span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></s></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>其中：</span><span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span lang=EN-US>currentValue</span></i><i
style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>获取的是控件对应保存到数据库的值（当总为字符串，对于多选下拉框控件，值为所选中项的值以双冒号</span><span
lang=EN-US>::</span></i><i style='mso-bidi-font-style:normal'><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>分隔组合而成）。</span><span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></i></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt'>4.1.5 </span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>子表单内的表达式特殊规则</span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri'>规则一、（前端）通过表单引擎，使用</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%'>&quot;@@&quot;</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri'>前缀（</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'>@@</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>表示当前表单界面）获取当前子表单对话框内控件值，因此如果在主表单内也写有此前缀时，应忽略（就好象没有此前缀一样，因为此时当前表单界面就是主表单），这样可以保证表单单独使用时，控件的表达式运算不会出错。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.25pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.02;
line-height:150%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>比如对话框包括两个字段</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'>“JOB_S1.FA”</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>、</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'>“JOB_S1.FB”</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，此时在</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'>FA</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri'>字段内定义了验证表达式，需要获取</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:150%'>FB</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>的字段值时，使用如下方式取值：</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:150%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt'>var
fbVal=$.F.getFieldValue(&quot;@@JOB_S1.FB&quot;);<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>规则二、在调用</span><span lang=EN-US>$.F.setFieldValue</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>保存子表单控件值时，需要对每条记录验证，通过</span><span
lang=EN-US>$.Data[&quot;currRecord&quot;]</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>传入当前表单数据。而</span><span
lang=EN-US>$.F.getFieldValue</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>获取有</span><span lang=EN-US>@@</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>前缀字段值时，从此属性所传入的记录对象中获取（如果此属性无效，则按规则一从表单界面获取值）。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>但需要考虑子表单嵌套。</span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>规则三（扩展）、前缀名为“</span><span lang=EN-US>@n@</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体'>”</span><span style='font-family:宋体'>（其中<span
lang=EN-US>n</span>为层次数）表示是当前子表单父表单引用。如果<span lang=EN-US>n</span>已大于当前子表单的层次数，则总为主表单。比如：业务表单的<span
lang=EN-US>JOB_A.F1</span>是子表单控件，关联表单包含名为<span lang=EN-US>JOB_B.F11</span>的子表单控件，其关联表单包含名为<span
lang=EN-US>JOB_C.F111</span>的输入控件，在此控件上定义计算表达式时：<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体'>var x0=$.F.getFieldValue(&quot;@@JOB_C.F112&quot;);
//</span><span style='font-family:宋体'>与当前控件（<span lang=EN-US>JOB_C.F111</span>）同一表单内<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体'>var x1=$.F.getFieldValue(&quot;@1@JOB_C.F12&quot;);
//</span><span style='font-family:宋体'>当前控件所在表单的直接父表单<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体'>var x2=$.F.getFieldValue(&quot;@2@JOB_C.F2&quot;);
//</span><span style='font-family:宋体'>当前控件所在表单的上两层的父表单（这里是主表单）<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-family:宋体'>var x3=$.F.getFieldValue(&quot;@3@JOB_C.F2&quot;);
//</span><span style='font-family:宋体'>当前控件所在表单的上三层的父表单（因为这里没有三层，也是指主表）<span
lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:14.0pt'>4.1.6 </span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:14.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>代码书写入门</span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:14.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></b></p>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0

 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:0;mso-yfti-firstrow:yes'>
  <td width=385 valign=top style='width:288.9pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>代码段</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=227 valign=top style='width:6.0cm;border:solid black 1.0pt;

  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>function Func(v1,v2){</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> 
  </span>return v1+v2;</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>}</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=227 valign=top style='width:6.0cm;border-top:none;border-left:none;

  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>定义一个函数</span></p>
  </td>

 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:2'>

  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>var data=[1,2,3,4,5];</span></p>

  <td width=227 valign=top style='width:6.0cm;border-top:none;border-left:none;

  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>定义一个数组</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:3'>
  <td width=385 valign=top style='width:288.9pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;

  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>typeof(obj);</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=227 valign=top style='width:6.0cm;border-top:none;border-left:none;

  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>获取对象类型的字符串描述。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>通用类型：</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='color:red'>undefined</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri;color:red'>、</span><span lang=EN-US style='color:red'>object</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri;color:red'>、</span><span lang=EN-US style='color:red'>function</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>以及具体的值类型：</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>string</span><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>、</span><span

  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>、</span><span lang=EN-US>boolean</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>(</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>注：值为</span><span
  lang=EN-US>null</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，类型为</span><span lang=EN-US>object)</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:4'>
  <td width=385 valign=top style='width:288.9pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;

  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>var filtered=data.filter( function(i){return
  i%2==0;}, 0);</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=227 valign=top style='width:6.0cm;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:

  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;

  </td>

 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:5'>
  <td width=385 valign=top style='width:288.9pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;

  </span>time: new Date()</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>};</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=227 valign=top style='width:6.0cm;border-top:none;border-left:none;

  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>构造一个对象，含</span><span lang=EN-US>foo</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>、</span><span lang=EN-US>time</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>属性</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:6'>
  <td width=385 valign=top style='width:288.9pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;

  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>} catch(e){</span></p>

  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>}</span></p>
  </td>

  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>捕获异常</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:7'>
  <td width=385 valign=top style='width:288.9pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>var abc = function(){</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>         </span><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>if(true){</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>         </span><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>    </span>return 'aaa';</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>         </span><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>}else{</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>         </span><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>    </span>return 'bb';</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>         </span><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>}</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span style='mso-tab-count:1'>         </span>}</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US><span
  style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>abc();</span></p>
  </td>
  <td width=227 valign=top style='width:6.0cm;border-top:none;border-left:none;
  border-bottom:solid black 1.0pt;border-right:solid black 1.0pt;mso-border-top-alt:
  solid black .5pt;mso-border-left-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>根据不同情况，当需要返回值时，应当将代码块，写在一个方法里。</span></p>
  </td>
 </tr>
 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:8'>
  <td width=385 valign=top style='width:288.9pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;
  border-top:none;mso-border-top-alt:solid black .5pt;mso-border-alt:solid black .5pt;
  padding:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt'>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan;tab-stops:183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt;
  background:#F7F7F7'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.0pt;font-family:宋体;
  mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:#454545;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>var HashMap =
  Java.type(&quot;java.util.HashMap&quot;);<o:p></o:p></span></p>

 <tr style='mso-yfti-irow:13'>
  <td width=385 valign=top style='width:288.9pt;border:solid black 1.0pt;

  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>var o1 = {age: 15};</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US>var o2 = {name: 'bar'};</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt;
  background:#F7F7F7'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.0pt;font-family:宋体;

  o2);<span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>   </span></span><span lang=EN-US
  style='font-size:9.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:#538135;
  mso-font-kerning:0pt'>//</span><span style='font-size:9.0pt;font-family:宋体;
  mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:#538135;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>绑定<span
  lang=EN-US>o2</span>到<span lang=EN-US>o1</span>上<span lang=EN-US><o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt;
  background:#F7F7F7'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.0pt;font-family:宋体;
  mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:#454545;mso-font-kerning:0pt'>print('</span><span

  mso-font-kerning:0pt'>对象的<span lang=EN-US>o1</span>属性：<span lang=EN-US>' +
  o1.name + ', ' + o1.age);<o:p></o:p></span></span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt;

  15<o:p></o:p></span></span></p>

  <p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
  normal'><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri;color:#0070C0'>服务端脚本有效。</span></b><span lang=EN-US>load</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>外部</span><span lang=EN-US>JS</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>文件。</span></p>
  <p class=MsoNormal align=left style='text-align:left'><span style='font-family:
  宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>如果加载的</span><span
  lang=EN-US>js</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
  mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>文件中可能存在重名的变量，导致被覆盖时，可以使用</span><span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.0pt'>oadWithNewGlobal('xx.js', arg1,arg2,...);</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>方法加载到一个新的上下文中执行。其中的</span><span lang=EN-US>arg</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>参数传入并通过新上下文的全局变量</span><span lang=EN-US>arguments</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>访问</span><span lang=EN-US>(arguments[0]</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>是</span><span lang=EN-US>arg1</span><span style='font-family:宋体;
  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>参数值，</span><span
  lang=EN-US>arguments[1]</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
  Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>是</span><span lang=EN-US>arg2</span><span
  style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
  Calibri'>参数值，依次类推。</span></p>
  </td>

  lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.0pt;color:#454545'>var runner = new Runner() {<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre

  lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.0pt;color:#454545'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span>run: function() {<o:p></o:p></span></pre><pre

  style='text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:#F7F7F7'><span

  style='font-size:9.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-bidi-font-family:宋体;color:#538135;

  <p class=MsoNormal style='mso-pagination:widow-orphan;tab-stops:45.8pt 91.6pt 137.4pt 183.2pt 229.0pt 274.8pt 320.6pt 366.4pt 412.2pt 458.0pt 503.8pt 549.6pt 595.4pt 641.2pt 687.0pt 732.8pt;

  <pre style='text-align:justify;text-justify:inter-ideograph;background:#F7F7F7'><span
  lang=EN-US style='font-size:9.0pt;color:#454545'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></pre></td>

  mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>通过全局属性输出调试信息</span><span
