<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:red'>注</span><span lang=EN-US
style='color:red'>1</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri;color:red'>：</span><span lang=EN-US>javascript</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>内非基本对象返回给</span><span
lang=EN-US>java</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>类时，都将封装为</span><span lang=EN-US>ScriptObjectMirror</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>对象返回，而对于集合，将总是</span><span
lang=EN-US>Map</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>类型（即使</span><span lang=EN-US>javascript</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>内部定义的是数组对象）。因此，如果</span><span
lang=EN-US>java</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>类需要的是数组或列表时，要么将</span><span lang=EN-US>JS</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>数组转为</span><span
lang=EN-US>Java</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>的</span><span lang=EN-US>List</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>对象；要么返回</span><span
lang=EN-US>JSON</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>字符串，由调用者再转换为</span><span lang=EN-US>List</span><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>。</span></p>

<h2 style='margin-left:1.0cm;text-indent:-1.0cm;mso-list:l4 level2 lfo1'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>4.3.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria'>接口及功能实现</span></h2>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>接口名：</span><span lang=EN-US>interface<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>ISnBuilderService<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>类名：</span><span lang=EN-US>class<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>SnBuilderService</b></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:
14.4pt;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:
Calibri'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>1)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>List&lt;SerialExpFla&gt;<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='color:#0070C0'>findAll </span></b>()<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【描述】获取所有编号表达式</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【参数】无</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【返回】所有的编号表达式。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:
14.4pt;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:
Calibri'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>2)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>SerialExpFla<b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='color:#0070C0'> findOne </span></b>(String<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span><span style='color:red'>rid</span>)<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【描述】根据</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;color:red'>rid</span><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>获取编号表达式</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【参数】</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:35.4pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.95;
line-height:14.4pt'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;color:red'>rid</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，编号表达式的唯一标识符。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【返回】指定的编号表达式对象，如果不存在，返回</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>null</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:
14.4pt;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:
Calibri'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>3)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>List&lt;SerialExpFla&gt;<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='color:#0070C0'>findByName </span></b>(String<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span><span style='color:red'>name</span>)<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【描述】根据指定编号表达式名称查找编号</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【参数】</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:35.4pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.95;
line-height:14.4pt'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;color:red'>name</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，编号表达式名称。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【返回】如果找到，返回指定的编号表达式，否则返回空集合。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:
14.4pt;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US

Calibri'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>4)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>String<span

serialExpFla</span>)<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;

lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:35.4pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.95;

style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，编号表达式对象。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【返回】新添加的编号表达式对象的标识码。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:115%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;

Calibri'>【实现】</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>注意，</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>serialExpFla</span><span style='font-size:
12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>中</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>rid</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>不被使用，相反，程序会自动生成一个</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>rid</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>作为主键</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

14.4pt;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:
Calibri'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>5)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>void<span

serialExpFla</span>)<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;

style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，要修改的编号表达式对象。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;

</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>void<span

</span><span style='color:red'>rid</span>)<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:35.4pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.95;

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span lang=EN-US

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:
14.4pt;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:
Calibri'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>7)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>void<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='color:#0070C0'>deleteByName </span></b>(String<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span><span style='color:red'>name</span>)<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【描述】根据指定编号表达式名称删除编号公式</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【参数】</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:35.4pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.95;
line-height:14.4pt'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;color:red'>name</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，编号公式名称。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【返回】无</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:115%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri'>【实现】如果数据库中不存在这一条记录，这个方法会抛出异常</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:115%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt;text-indent:-18.0pt;line-height:
14.4pt;mso-list:l2 level1 lfo2'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:
Calibri'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>8)<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>String<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='color:#0070C0'>eval</span></b>(String <span style='color:red'>rid</span>,
IFormService <span style='color:red'>formService</span>)<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【描述】计算表达式</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【参数】</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:35.4pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.95;
line-height:14.4pt'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;color:red'>Rid</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，表达式对象标识符。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:35.4pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.95;
line-height:14.4pt'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;color:red'>formService</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>，表单对象</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:14.4pt'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>【返回】生成的编号公式。</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h2 style='margin-left:1.0cm;text-indent:-1.0cm;mso-list:l4 level2 lfo1'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Cambria;mso-bidi-font-family:Cambria'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>4.4.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Cambria;mso-hansi-font-family:Cambria'>服务实现</span></h2>

<h3><span lang=EN-US>4.2.1</span><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>．通用说明</span></h3>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>类名：</span><span lang=EN-US>class<span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'>  </span><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>SnBuilderController<o:p></o:p></b></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:21.25pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.77;
line-height:115%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>服务调用仅对功能实现类进行了简单封装，通用的处理都是：①从“请求”对象中获取需要的参数，②并进行转换以适合功能类的调用，③通过注入得到功能类对象，④调用其相应方法，⑤在得到结果后写入到“回应”对象中，⑥如果出错，向“回应”对象写入</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>5xx</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>错误信息。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:21.25pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.77;
line-height:115%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>服务方法定义格式如下：</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>void </span><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='color:#0070C0'>MethodName</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt'>(String <span style='color:red'>sParam1</span>,
String <span style='color:red'>dtParam2</span>, …,<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:18.0pt'><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt'><span style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span><span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>HttpServletRequest <span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span><span style='color:red'>request</span>, <span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span>HttpServletResponse <span
style='mso-spacerun:yes'> </span><span style='color:red'>response</span>)<o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.25pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.02;
line-height:115%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>框架会自动做一些工作，从请求对象中得到需要的参数；<b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>对于无法通过简单类型映射成参数的，可以在代码中直接操作</b></span><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:115%'>request</span></b><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>来得到需要的参数。</span></b><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.25pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.02;
line-height:115%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>调用对应注入对象的方法，并得到结果。<b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'>如果方法调用出错，会抛出异常。</b></span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.25pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.02;
line-height:115%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>将结果写入到回应（</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>response</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>）对象中，<b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'>简单类型将直接返回，其它复杂类型（如自定义类）则序列化为</b></span><b style='mso-bidi-font-weight:
normal'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>json</span></b><b
style='mso-bidi-font-weight:normal'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>串返回。</span></b><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:24.25pt;mso-char-indent-count:2.02;
line-height:115%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>如果出现异常，返回</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>5xx</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>错误（错误内容可视情况设置）。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='text-indent:21.25pt;mso-char-indent-count:1.77;
line-height:115%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:
宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>每个方法具有的参数及返回格式，参见第</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>7</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>节服务方式调用的说明。</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<h1 style='margin-left:21.25pt;text-indent:-21.25pt;mso-list:l4 level1 lfo1'><![if !supportLists]><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-fareast-font-family:Calibri;mso-bidi-font-family:Calibri'><span
style='mso-list:Ignore'>5.<span style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp;&nbsp;
</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>数据库表设计</span></h1>

<p class=MsoNormal><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;
mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>编号公式对象表</span></p>

<table class=MsoNormalTable border=1 cellspacing=0 cellpadding=0
 style='border-collapse:collapse;border:none;mso-border-alt:solid windowtext .5pt;
 mso-padding-alt:0cm 5.4pt 0cm 5.4pt;mso-border-insideh:.5pt solid windowtext;

</span></span></span><![endif]><span style='font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:

<p class=MsoNormal style='margin-left:0cm;text-indent:0cm;line-height:115%;
mso-list:l3 level1 lfo3'><![if !supportLists]><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:Wingdings;mso-fareast-font-family:
Wingdings;mso-bidi-font-family:Wingdings'><span style='mso-list:Ignore'>Ø<span
style='font:7.0pt "Times New Roman"'>&nbsp; </span></span></span><![endif]><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>以接口方式调用的注入配置说明</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:115%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri'>方式一：在类实现中，以注解的方式定义了名为“</span><span lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:
10.5pt;line-height:115%'>snbuilder</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:115%'>Service</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri'>”的注入对象。</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
115%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:115%'><span style='font-size:12.0pt;
line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:
Calibri'>方式二：引入“</span><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
115%'>snbuilderService.jar</span><span style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:
115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>”及“</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>snbuilderServiceInterface.jar</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体'>”</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>包，构造类对象“</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>com.southgis.ibase. </span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:115%'>snbuilder</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>.service. </span><span
lang=EN-US style='mso-bidi-font-size:10.5pt;line-height:115%'>SnBuilder</span><span
lang=EN-US style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'>Service</span><span
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%;font-family:宋体;mso-ascii-font-family:
Calibri;mso-hansi-font-family:Calibri'>”</span><span lang=EN-US
style='font-size:12.0pt;line-height:115%'><o:p></o:p></span></p>

<p class=MsoNormal style='line-height:115%'><span lang=EN-US style='font-size:
12.0pt;line-height:115%'><o:p>&nbsp;</o:p></span></p>
